<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привезти.html>привезти́</a> (1249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привезти.html>привезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привозить.html>привози́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring, to fetch by vehicle ((transitive) to transport toward somebody/somewhere)</li></ol>

***привередливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привередливый.html>привере́дливый</a> (29575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вере́дливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">verédlivyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak, effeminate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ве́ред</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véred</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boil, abscess</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, where <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ве́ред</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> originally meant, and still dialectally means, "pain, harm"; compare doublet <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вред.html>вред</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Sense development "too sensitive to pain" → "weak, effeminate" → "squeamish, picky".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привередливый.html>привере́дливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priverédlivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>picky, choosy, hard to please, fastidious, squeamish, excessively particular</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привередливый.html>привере́дливо</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priverédlivo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привере́дливость</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priverédlivostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привереда</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">privereda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привередник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priverednik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привередница</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priverednica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привередничать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priveredničatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привередничание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priveredničanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привередничество</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priveredničestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привести.html>привести́</a> (632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привести.html>привести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone with</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to lead <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a road</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to result, to lead, to bring</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reduce</li>
<li>to quote, to cite, to adduce, to list</li>
<li>to bring, to put, to set <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">into condition</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***привет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привет.html>приве́т</a> (2187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">привѣтъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privětŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">greeting; appeal; dictum, word; intention, will; ?</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*privětъ</i>.
</p>

</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привет.html>приве́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привет.html>приве́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привет.html>приве́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привет.html>приве́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a greeting, a hello</li></ol>

***приветствовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приветствовать.html>приве́тствовать</a> (4021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приветствовать.html>приве́тствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privétstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поприветствовать.html>поприве́тствовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to greet, to hail, to welcome</li>
<li>to salute</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́т<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ство<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привечать.html>привеча́ть</a> (30336)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — приветить.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-привеч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***прививать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прививать.html>привива́ть</a> (23782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прививать.html>привива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to inoculate, to vaccinate <i>(against)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to engraft <i>(upon)</i>, to inoculate <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><i>(a habit or property)</i> to inculcate, to impart, to cultivate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прививать.html>привива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:практический.html>практи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:навык.html>на́выки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privivátʹ</b> praktíčeskije návyki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impart practical skills</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прививать.html>привива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́тям</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privivátʹ</b> détjam ljubóvʹ k trudú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cultivate/implant/foster love for/of work in children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прививать.html>привива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мода.html>мо́ду</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> )</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privivátʹ</b> nóvuju módu (na )</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set a new fashion (for, in)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">частичн.</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:приспосабливать.html>приспоса́бливать</a>, акклиматизировать</li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произношение.html>произноше́ния</a>: привиденье.

***привилегированный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привилегированный.html>привилегиро́ванный</a> (16680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Constructed as a past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*привилегирова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*privilegirovátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to privilege</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a> (16831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прививать.html>привива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to inoculate, to vaccinate <i>(against)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to engraft <i>(upon)</i>, to inoculate <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><i>(a habit or property)</i> to inculcate, to impart, to cultivate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:практический.html>практи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:навык.html>на́выки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privítʹ</b> praktíčeskije návyki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impart practical skills</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́тям</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privítʹ</b> détjam ljubóvʹ k trudú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cultivate/implant/foster love for/of work in children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привить.html>приви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мода.html>мо́ду</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> )</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privítʹ</b> nóvuju módu (na )</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set a new fashion (for, in)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привкус.html>при́вкус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prívkus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привкус.html>при́вкуса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привкус.html>при́вкусы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привкус.html>при́вкусов</a></b>)

<ol><li>smack, touch, aftertaste

<li>shade, tinge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внести.html>внести́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привкус.html>при́вкус</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скептицизм.html>скептици́зма</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vnestí <b>prívkus</b> skepticízma</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">introduce a tinge of skepticism</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привлёкший.html>привлёкший</a> (3241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привлёкший.html>привлёкший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privljókšij</span>)
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>привлека́тельнее, привлека́тельней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-влек-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-тельн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to attract, to draw <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">arouse interest</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>привод</a> (17393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, since the 19th century. Perhaps a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Antrieb</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́д</a><sup>*</sup></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prívod</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privód<sup>*</sup></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вода</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́да</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>привода́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́ды</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приводо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́дов</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приводно́й</b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Alternative, non-professional-only usage.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
